# <a name="office-client-application-and-platform-availability-for-office-add-ins"></a><span data-ttu-id="a75ea-103">Disponibilidade de aplicativos e plataformas do cliente Office para Suplementos do Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-103">Office client application and platform availability for Office Add-ins</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a75ea-104">Seu Suplemento do Office pode depender de um aplicativo específico do Office, um conjunto de requisitos, um membro de API ou uma versão da API para funcionar conforme o esperado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-104">To work as expected, your Office Add-in might depend on a specific Office application, a requirement set, an API member, or a version of the API.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a75ea-105">As tabelas a seguir contêm as plataformas disponíveis, os pontos de extensão, os conjuntos de requisitos de API e os conjuntos de requisitos comuns de API que são compatíveis atualmente com cada aplicativo do Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-105">The following tables contain the available platforms, extension points, API requirement sets, and Common APIs that are currently supported for each Office application.</span></span>

<br>

|<a href="#excel"><img src="../images/index/logo-excel.svg" alt="Excel" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="a75ea-106"><span>Excel</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-106"><span>Excel</span></a></span></span>|<a href="#onenote"><img src="../images/index/logo-onenote.svg" alt="OneNote" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="a75ea-107"><span>OneNote</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-107"><span>OneNote</span></a></span></span>|<a href="#outlook"><img src="../images/index/logo-outlook.svg" alt="Outlook" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="a75ea-108"><span>Outlook</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-108"><span>Outlook</span></a></span></span>|<a href="#powerpoint"><img src="../images/index/logo-powerpoint.svg" alt="PowerPoint" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="a75ea-109"><span>PowerPoint</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-109"><span>PowerPoint</span></a></span></span>|<a href="#project"><img src="../images/index/logo-project-server.svg" alt="Project" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="a75ea-110"><span>Project</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-110"><span>Project</span></a></span></span>|<a href="#word"><img src="../images/index/logo-word.svg" alt="Word" width="48" /><br><span data-ttu-id="a75ea-111"><span>Word</span></a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-111"><span>Word</span></a></span></span>|
|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="a75ea-112">A versão inicial do Office 2016 instalada por meio do MSI apenas contém os conjuntos de requisitos ExcelApi 1.1, WordApi 1.1 e os conjuntos de requisitos comuns de API.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-112">The initial Office 2016 release installed via MSI only contains the ExcelApi 1.1, WordApi 1.1, and Common API requirement sets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a75ea-113">Para saber mais sobre o histórico de atualizações de várias versões do Office, confira a seção[Confira também](#see-also).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-113">For more information about the update history of the various Office versions, check out the [See also](#see-also) section.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="a75ea-563"><sup>1</sup> Para exigir o conjunto 1.3 da API de Identidade no código do suplemento, verifique se ele tem suporte ligando para `isSetSupported('IdentityAPI', '1.3')`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-563"><sup>1</sup> To require Identity API set 1.3 in your add-in code, check if it's supported by calling `isSetSupported('IdentityAPI', '1.3')`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a75ea-564">Não há suporte para declará-lo no manifesto do seu suplemento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-564">Declaring it in your add-in's manifest isn't supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a75ea-565">Você também pode determinar se a API tem suporte, verificando se ela não é `undefined`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-565">You can also determine if the API is supported by checking that it's not `undefined`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a75ea-566">Para mais detalhes, confira [Usar APIs de conjuntos de requisitos posteriores](../reference/requirement-sets/outlook-api-requirement-sets.md#using-apis-from-later-requirement-sets).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-566">For further details, see [Using APIs from later requirement sets](../reference/requirement-sets/outlook-api-requirement-sets.md#using-apis-from-later-requirement-sets).</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="a75ea-567"><sup>2</sup> Adicionado com atualizações pós-lançamento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-567"><sup>2</sup> Added with post-release updates.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="a75ea-568"><sup>3</sup> O suporte para a nova Interface do Usuário do Mac (visualização) está disponível no Outlook versão 16.38.506.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-568"><sup>3</sup> Support for the new Mac UI (preview) is available from Outlook version 16.38.506.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a75ea-569">Para mais informações, consulte a seção [Suporte de Suplemento no Outlook na nova Interface do Usuário do Mac](../outlook/compare-outlook-add-in-support-in-outlook-for-mac.md#add-in-support-in-outlook-on-new-mac-ui-preview).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-569">For more information, see the [Add-in support in Outlook on new Mac UI](../outlook/compare-outlook-add-in-support-in-outlook-for-mac.md#add-in-support-in-outlook-on-new-mac-ui-preview) section.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="a75ea-570">O suporte ao cliente para um conjunto de requisitos pode ser restringido pelo suporte do servidor Exchange.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-570">Client support for a requirement set may be restricted by Exchange server support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a75ea-571">Consulte [Conjuntos de requisitos da API JavaScript do Outlook](../reference/requirement-sets/outlook-api-requirement-sets.md#requirement-sets-supported-by-exchange-servers-and-outlook-clients) para obter detalhes sobre o intervalo de conjuntos de requisitos suportado pelo servidor Exchange e pelos clientes Outlook.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a75ea-571">See [Outlook JavaScript API requirement sets](../reference/requirement-sets/outlook-api-requirement-sets.md#requirement-sets-supported-by-exchange-servers-and-outlook-clients) for details about the range of requirement sets supported by Exchange server and Outlook clients.</span></span>
